The rack has 7 letters, shared by all participants.\r\n\r\nEach player has their own color : red (1st player) and then green, blue and yellow.\r\n\r\nSuppose that you are the \"red\" player : when your words reuse tiles already placed by an opponent, all these tiles become red.
